<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Records_and_statistics">Records and statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_Club_World_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Records and statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tmulti tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:204px;max-width:204px">
<div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:202px;max-width:202px">
<div class="thumbimage"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lionel_Messi_at_Bernabeu.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="1648" data-file-width="819" height="402" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Lionel_Messi_at_Bernabeu.jpg/200px-Lionel_Messi_at_Bernabeu.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Lionel_Messi_at_Bernabeu.jpg/300px-Lionel_Messi_at_Bernabeu.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Lionel_Messi_at_Bernabeu.jpg/400px-Lionel_Messi_at_Bernabeu.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a></div>
<div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left"><a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> is the joint all-time leading goalscorer of the tournament along with <a href="/wiki/Luis_Su%C3%A1rez" title="Luis Suárez">Luis Suárez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> and <a href="/wiki/C%C3%A9sar_Delgado" title="César Delgado">César Delgado</a></div>
</div>
<div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:202px;max-width:202px">
<div class="thumbimage"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Guardiola_2010.jpg"><img alt="Josep Guardiola is seen in the picture. He is shown with a faded beard and hair wearing a suit." data-file-height="591" data-file-width="600" height="197" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Guardiola_2010.jpg/200px-Guardiola_2010.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Guardiola_2010.jpg/300px-Guardiola_2010.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Guardiola_2010.jpg/400px-Guardiola_2010.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a></div>
<div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left"><a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a> is the most successful manager, winning two of his titles with Barcelona and a third with <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Club_World_Cup_records_and_statistics" title="FIFA Club World Cup records and statistics">FIFA Club World Cup records and statistics</a></div>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_goalscorers" title="List of FIFA Club World Cup goalscorers">List of FIFA Club World Cup goalscorers</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_winning_managers" title="List of FIFA Club World Cup winning managers">List of FIFA Club World Cup winning managers</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Historical_table_of_the_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="Historical table of the FIFA Club World Cup">Historical table of the FIFA Club World Cup</a></div>
<p>Seven players have won the FIFA Club World Cup on three occasions: <a href="/wiki/Dani_Alves" title="Dani Alves">Dani Alves</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[160]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Busquets" title="Sergio Busquets">Sergio Busquets</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170"><a href="#cite_note-170">[161]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Iniesta" title="Andrés Iniesta">Andrés Iniesta</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Andres_Iniesta_171-0"><a href="#cite_note-Andres_Iniesta-171">[162]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lionel_Messi_101-1"><a href="#cite_note-Lionel_Messi-101">[101]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Gerard_Piqu%C3%A9" title="Gerard Piqué">Gerard Piqué</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172"><a href="#cite_note-172">[163]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cristiano_Ronaldo_173-0"><a href="#cite_note-Cristiano_Ronaldo-173">[164]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Toni_Kroos" title="Toni Kroos">Toni Kroos</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174"><a href="#cite_note-174">[165]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/C%C3%A9sar_Delgado" title="César Delgado">César Delgado</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luis_Su%C3%A1rez" title="Luis Suárez">Luis Suárez</a> hold the record of being the <a href="/wiki/List_of_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_goalscorers" title="List of FIFA Club World Cup goalscorers">overall top goalscorers in FIFA Club World Cup history</a> with five goals.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175"><a href="#cite_note-175">[166]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Denilson_Martins_Nascimento" title="Denilson Martins Nascimento">Denilson</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Aboutrika" title="Mohamed Aboutrika">Mohamed Aboutrika</a> share fifth place with four goals each.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lionel_Messi_101-2"><a href="#cite_note-Lionel_Messi-101">[101]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Denilson_176-0"><a href="#cite_note-Denilson-176">[167]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177"><a href="#cite_note-177">[168]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Wael_Gomaa" title="Wael Gomaa">Wael Gomaa</a> is the player with most appearances in the competition with eleven matches, followed by Xavi, Valdés and Puyol playing six matches each.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Andres_Iniesta_171-1"><a href="#cite_note-Andres_Iniesta-171">[162]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Puyol_178-0"><a href="#cite_note-Puyol-178">[169]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Valdes_179-0"><a href="#cite_note-Valdes-179">[170]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Xavi_180-0"><a href="#cite_note-Xavi-180">[171]</a></sup></p>
<p>Barcelona claims the record with the most wins (7).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Overview_110-1"><a href="#cite_note-Overview-110">[110]</a></sup> Corinthians, Necaxa, Real Madrid and <a href="/wiki/Kashiwa_Reysol" title="Kashiwa Reysol">Kashiwa Reysol</a> have the most draws (2), while <a href="/wiki/Al_Ahly_SC" title="Al Ahly SC">Al Ahly</a> have the record of the most losses (7).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Overview_110-2"><a href="#cite_note-Overview-110">[110]</a></sup> Barcelona also possess the record for most goals scored in the competition (23), while Al Ahly claim the record of most goals conceded (15).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Overview_110-3"><a href="#cite_note-Overview-110">[110]</a></sup> Barcelona also has the best goal difference in the competition (+20).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Overview_110-4"><a href="#cite_note-Overview-110">[110]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a> is the only head coach to win three FIFA Club World Cups.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Overview_110-5"><a href="#cite_note-Overview-110">[110]</a></sup></p>
<p>As of the end of the 2016 tournament, Auckland City has played the most games with 14 in eight different tournaments. Barcelona holds the record for scoring the most goals, playing eight games in four different editions and scoring 23 goals.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Overview_110-6"><a href="#cite_note-Overview-110">[110]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Reception">Reception</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_Club_World_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Reception">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Since its inception in 2000, the competition, despite its name and the contestants' achievements, has received differing reception. In most of Europe it struggles to find broad media attention compared to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> and commonly lacks recognition as a high-ranking contest.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-181"><a href="#cite_note-181">[172]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-182"><a href="#cite_note-182">[173]</a></sup> In South America, however, it is widely considered the highest point in the career of a footballer, coach and/or team at international club level.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183"><a href="#cite_note-183">[174]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184"><a href="#cite_note-184">[175]</a></sup></p>
<p>The competition is also criticized, mainly by the European press and fans among others, by its competition format, which widely favours the UEFA and CONMEBOL teams, since their contestants start in the semi-final round and can only play between them in the final match. It is also criticized for its poor organisation, the poor reception among the local fans for the matches not featuring any European or South American team, FIFA's decision to select the competition's host based on economic deals and not on their footballing merit at the international stage like <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a>, and the poor economic benefits for the winning team, regarded as inferior than any <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Super_Cup" title="Super Cup">Super Cup</a> prizes.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185"><a href="#cite_note-185">[176]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-186"><a href="#cite_note-186">[177]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_Club_World_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em; list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">

<li id="cite_note-151"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-151">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">No extra time was played in the third-place match. Atlético Nacional won 4–3 on penalties.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[142]</a></sup></span></li>
</ol>
</div>

<li id="cite_note-29"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-29">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://hemeroteca.mundodeportivo.com/preview/1967/11/03/pagina-6/936416/pdf.html" rel="nofollow">/Mundo Deportivo. <li id="cite_note-30"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-30">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="https://news.google.com/newspapers?nid=GGgVawPscysC&amp;dat=19671106&amp;printsec=frontpage&amp;hl=pt-BR" rel="nofollow">Glasgow Herald (Scottish newspaper, 06/Nov/1967, page 06: "Sir Stanley said then that FIFA regarded the competition, which is between the winners of the European Cup and the South American equivalent, as a friendly fixture".</a></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-31"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-31">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://www.archiviolastampa.it/component/option,com_lastampa/task,ricerche/Itemid,3/" rel="nofollow">Archive of Italian newspaper La Stampa. Look for: "La finale mondiale Europa-America di calcio ufficialmente è una semplice gara amichevole", published 03.nov.1967 page 10."</a></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-32"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-32">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://hemeroteca.abc.es/nav/Navigate.exe/hemeroteca/madrid/abc/1967/11/03/097.html" rel="nofollow">ABC Newspaper, Madrid (Spain), Nov. 03, 1967, page 97. Headline <i>La FIFA no quiere saber nada de la final intercontinental, pues para ella es um partido "amistoso"</i>. (In English: FIFA does not care about the Intercontinental final, as, for FIFA, it is a "friendly match".) Contents in Spanish: <i>Rous declaró em um almuerzo de redactores esportivos que los partidos anuales para el título intercontinental – entre los ganadores de la Copa de Europa y de America del Sur – está considerados oficialmente como encontros amistosos. .... Rous anadió que otras Federaciones, la Asiatica y de Americas Central y del Norte – han solicitado la participacion de sus clubs campeones en la Copa Intercontinental . Se oponen a ello – dijo el – las federaciones Europea y Sudamericana ... Siguió diciendo Sir Stanley que espera que se estudie todo lo relacionado con la competicion en la proxima Asemblea General de la FIFA: "Si se aprueba, la competicion se desarrollaria a partir de entonces bajo la tutela del organismo mundial que presido", finalizó diciendo Sir Stanley Rous</i> ... (English translation: Rous stated, during a lunch with sports writers, that the annual matches for the intercontinental cup – between the winners of the European Cup and the South American one- are officially considered as friendly fixtures ... Rous also said that other Federations, the Asian and the North-Central American one- have requested the participation of their champion clubs in the Intercontinental Cup. According to Rous, the European and South American federations are opposed to it ... Sir Stanley kept on saying that he expects that everything related to the competition should be studied in the next FIFA General Assembly: "If approved, the competition would go on from then on under the auspices of the world organisation I preside", concluded Sir Stanley.)</a></span></li>
